NetPrem
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 16
row: 9
value: =IF([TransType]="LS", [OpnPrem]+[ClsPrem],
                                            IF([TransType]="AS", [OpnPrem]+[ClsPrem],
                                               [OpnPrem]-[ClsPrem]))
--------------------
TotPrem
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 17
row: 9
value: =IF([SYM]="","",SUMIFS([NetPrem],[Trade'#],[[Trade'#]],[Leg],"<="&[Leg]))
--------------------
Days
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 18
row: 9
value: =IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="DEP",0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="DIV",0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="LS",TODAY() - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="AS",TODAY() - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE)>0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE)>0,INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),1),
INDIRECT("RC[-11]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE))))))
--------------------
Cap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 19
row: 9
value: =IF([TransType]="SP",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="LS",[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BP",100*([Strike]-[Strike2])*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BC",100*([Strike2]-[Strike])*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="NC",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="AS",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],0))))))
--------------------
OpenCap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 20
row: 9
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,"",[Cap])
--------------------
BEcap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 21
row: 9
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,"",
IF([TransType]="BC","",
IF([TransType]="BP",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
[Cap])))
--------------------
CapDays
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 22
row: 9
value: =IF([SYM]="","",[Cap]*[Days])
--------------------
TotCapDays
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 23
row: 9
value: =IF([SYM]="","",SUMIFS([CapDays],[Trade'#],[[Trade'#]],[Leg],"<="&[Leg]))
--------------------
AROI
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 24
row: 9
value: =IF([TotCapDays],365*[TotPrem]/[TotCapDays],"")
--------------------
BreakEven
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 25
row: 9
value: =IF([SYM]="","",
IF([TransType]="LS",[Strike]-[TotPrem]/[['#Contracts]],
IF([['#Contracts]],[Strike]-[TotPrem]/[['#Contracts]]/100,"")))
--------------------
ActShares
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 26
row: 9
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,"",
IF([TransType]="LS",['#Contracts],
IF([TransType]="AS",100*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="SP",100*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BP",100*[['#Contracts]],"")))))
--------------------
ActDate
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 27
row: 9
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,[CloseDate],
IF([ExpDate]>0,[ExpDate],
TODAY()))
--------------------
Inception
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 28
row: 9
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",[NetPrem]),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",[NetPrem]))
--------------------
1YR
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 29
row: 9
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8 - [ActDate]<366,[NetPrem],"")),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",
IF(TODAY() - [ActDate]<366,[NetPrem],"")))
--------------------
YTD
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 30
row: 9
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",
IF(YEAR(PERFORMANCE!D8)=YEAR([ActDate]),[NetPrem],"")),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",
IF(YEAR(TODAY())=YEAR([ActDate]),[NetPrem],"")))
--------------------
UnBooked
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 31
row: 9
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],[NetPrem],""),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],[NetPrem],""))
--------------------
TotPrem
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 33
row: 9
value: =IF(Table1[SYM]="","",SUMIFS(Table1[NetPrem],Table1[Trade'#],Table1[[Trade'#]],Table1[Leg],"<="&Table1[Leg]))
--------------------

sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 29
row: 20
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8 - [ActDate]<366,[NetPrem],"")),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",
IF(TODAY() - [ActDate]<366,[NetPrem],"")))
--------------------
YTD
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 30
row: 20
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",
IF(YEAR(PERFORMANCE!D8)=YEAR([ActDate]),[NetPrem],"")),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",
IF(YEAR(TODAY())=YEAR([ActDate]),[NetPrem],"")))
--------------------
UnBooked
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 31
row: 20
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],[NetPrem],""),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],[NetPrem],""))
--------------------
TotPrem
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 33
row: 20
value: =IF(Table1[SYM]="","",SUMIFS(Table1[NetPrem],Table1[Trade'#],Table1[[Trade'#]],Table1[Leg],"<="&Table1[Leg]))

TotPrem
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 17
row: 21
value: =IF([SYM]="","",SUMIFS([NetPrem],[Trade'#],[[Trade'#]],[Leg],"<="&[Leg]))
--------------------
Days
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 18
row: 21
value: =IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="DEP",0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="DIV",0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="LS",TODAY() - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="AS",TODAY() - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE)>0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE)>0,INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),1),
INDIRECT("RC[-11]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE))))))
--------------------
Cap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 19
row: 21
value: =IF([TransType]="SP",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="LS",[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BP",100*([Strike]-[Strike2])*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BC",100*([Strike2]-[Strike])*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="NC",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="AS",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],0))))))
--------------------
OpenCap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 20
row: 21
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,"",[Cap])
--------------------
BEcap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 21
row: 21
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,"",
IF([TransType]="BC","",
IF([TransType]="BP",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
[Cap])))
--------------------
CapDays
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 22
row: 21
value: =IF([SYM]="","",[Cap]*[Days])
--------------------
TotCapDays
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 23
row: 21
value: =IF([SYM]="","",SUMIFS([CapDays],[Trade'#],[[Trade'#]],[Leg],"<="&[Leg]))
--------------------
AROI
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 24
row: 21
value: =IF([TotCapDays],365*[TotPrem]/[TotCapDays],"")
--------------------
BreakEven
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 25
row: 21
value: =IF([SYM]="","",
IF([TransType]="LS",[Strike]-[TotPrem]/[['#Contracts]],
IF([['#Contracts]],[Strike]-[TotPrem]/[['#Contracts]]/100,"")))
--------------------
ActShares
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 26
row: 21
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,"",
IF([TransType]="LS",['#Contracts],
IF([TransType]="AS",100*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="SP",100*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BP",100*[['#Contracts]],"")))))
--------------------
ActDate
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">

row: 21
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,[CloseDate],
IF([ExpDate]>0,[ExpDate],
TODAY()))

currentAsk
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 15
row: 52
value: =RTD("tos.rtd",,"ASK",".PCAR210618P90")
--------------------
NetPrem
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 16
row: 52
value: =IF([TransType]="LS", [OpnPrem]+[ClsPrem],
                                            IF([TransType]="AS", [OpnPrem]+[ClsPrem],
                                               [OpnPrem]-[ClsPrem]))
--------------------
TotPrem
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 17
row: 52
value: =IF([SYM]="","",SUMIFS([NetPrem],[Trade'#],[[Trade'#]],[Leg],"<="&[Leg]))
--------------------
Days
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 18
row: 52
value: =IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="DEP",0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="DIV",0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="LS",TODAY() - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="AS",TODAY() - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE)>0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE)>0,INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),1),
INDIRECT("RC[-11]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE))))))
--------------------
Cap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 19
row: 52
value: =IF([TransType]="SP",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="LS",[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BP",100*([Strike]-[Strike2])*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BC",100*([Strike2]-[Strike])*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="NC",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="AS",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],0))))))
--------------------
OpenCap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 20
row: 52
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,"",[Cap])
--------------------
BEcap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 21
row: 52
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,"",
IF([TransType]="BC","",
IF([TransType]="BP",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
[Cap])))
--------------------
CapDays
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 22
row: 52
value: =IF([SYM]="","",[Cap]*[Days])
--------------------
TotCapDays
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 23
row: 52
value: =IF([SYM]="","",SUMIFS([CapDays],[Trade'#],[[Trade'#]],[Leg],"<="&[Leg]))
--------------------
AROI
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 24
row: 52
value: =IF([TotCapDays],365*[TotPrem]/[TotCapDays],"")
--------------------
BreakEven
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 25
row: 52
value: =IF([SYM]="","",
IF([TransType]="LS",[Strike]-[TotPrem]/[['#Contracts]],
IF([['#Contracts]],[Strike]-[TotPrem]/[['#Contracts]]/100,"")))
--------------------
ActShares
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 26
row: 52
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,"",
IF([TransType]="LS",['#Contracts],
IF([TransType]="AS",100*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="SP",100*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BP",100*[['#Contracts]],"")))))
--------------------
ActDate
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 27
row: 52
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,[CloseDate],
IF([ExpDate]>0,[ExpDate],
TODAY()))
--------------------
Inception
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 28
row: 52
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",[NetPrem]),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",[NetPrem]))
--------------------
1YR
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 29
row: 52
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8 - [ActDate]<366,[NetPrem],"")),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",
IF(TODAY() - [ActDate]<366,[NetPrem],"")))
--------------------
YTD
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 30
row: 52
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",
IF(YEAR(PERFORMANCE!D8)=YEAR([ActDate]),[NetPrem],"")),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",
IF(YEAR(TODAY())=YEAR([ActDate]),[NetPrem],"")))
--------------------
UnBooked
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 31
row: 52
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],[NetPrem],""),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],[NetPrem],""))
--------------------
TotPrem
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 33
row: 52
value: =IF(Table1[SYM]="","",SUMIFS(Table1[NetPrem],Table1[Trade'#],Table1[[Trade'#]],Table1[Leg],"<="&Table1[Leg]))

Days
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 18
row: 56
value: =IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="DEP",0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="DIV",0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="LS",TODAY() - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="AS",TODAY() - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE)>0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE)>0,INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),1),
INDIRECT("RC[-11]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE))))))
--------------------
Cap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 19
row: 56
value: =IF([TransType]="SP",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="LS",[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BP",100*([Strike]-[Strike2])*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BC",100*([Strike2]-[Strike])*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="NC",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="AS",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],0))))))
--------------------

[Cap])))

AROI

row: 56

row: 56

IF([['#Contracts]],[Strike]-[TotPrem]/[['#Contracts]]/100,"")))
--------------------

row: 56
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,"",
IF([TransType]="LS",['#Contracts],

IF([TransType]="BP",100*[['#Contracts]],"")))))

IF([ExpDate]>0,[ExpDate],

Inception
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 28
row: 56

IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",[NetPrem]))
--------------------
1YR
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 29
row: 56
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8 - [ActDate]<366,[NetPrem],"")),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",
IF(TODAY() - [ActDate]<366,[NetPrem],"")))
--------------------
YTD
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 30
row: 56
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",
IF(YEAR(PERFORMANCE!D8)=YEAR([ActDate]),[NetPrem],"")),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",
IF(YEAR(TODAY())=YEAR([ActDate]),[NetPrem],"")))
--------------------
UnBooked
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 31
row: 56
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,

IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],[NetPrem],""))

sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 18
row: 60
value: =IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="DEP",0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="DIV",0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="LS",TODAY() - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="AS",TODAY() - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE)>0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE)>0,INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),1),
INDIRECT("RC[-11]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE))))))

Cap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 19
row: 60
value: =IF([TransType]="SP",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="LS",[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BP",100*([Strike]-[Strike2])*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BC",100*([Strike2]-[Strike])*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="NC",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="AS",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],0))))))

[Cap])))

IF([TransType]="BP",100*[['#Contracts]],"")))))

Inception
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 28
row: 60

IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",[NetPrem]))
--------------------
1YR
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 29
row: 60
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8 - [ActDate]<366,[NetPrem],"")),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",
IF(TODAY() - [ActDate]<366,[NetPrem],"")))
--------------------
YTD
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 30
row: 60
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",
IF(YEAR(PERFORMANCE!D8)=YEAR([ActDate]),[NetPrem],"")),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",
IF(YEAR(TODAY())=YEAR([ActDate]),[NetPrem],"")))
--------------------
UnBooked
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 31
row: 60
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,

IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],[NetPrem],""))

row: 63
value: =IF(Table1[SYM]="","",SUMIFS(Table1[NetPrem],Table1[Trade'#],Table1[[Trade'#]],Table1[Leg],"<="&Table1[Leg]))

NetPrem

column: 16
row: 64
value: =IF([TransType]="LS", [OpnPrem]+[ClsPrem],
                                            IF([TransType]="AS", [OpnPrem]+[ClsPrem],
                                               [OpnPrem]-[ClsPrem]))
--------------------
TotPrem
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 17
row: 64
value: =IF([SYM]="","",SUMIFS([NetPrem],[Trade'#],[[Trade'#]],[Leg],"<="&[Leg]))
--------------------
Days
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 18
row: 64
value: =IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="DEP",0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="DIV",0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="LS",TODAY() - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-14]", FALSE)="AS",TODAY() - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE)>0,
IF(INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE)>0,INDIRECT("RC[-12]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE),1),
INDIRECT("RC[-11]", FALSE) - INDIRECT("RC[-13]", FALSE))))))
--------------------
Cap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 19
row: 64
value: =IF([TransType]="SP",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="LS",[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BP",100*([Strike]-[Strike2])*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BC",100*([Strike2]-[Strike])*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="NC",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="AS",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],0))))))
--------------------
OpenCap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 20
row: 64
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,"",[Cap])
--------------------
BEcap
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 21
row: 64
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,"",
IF([TransType]="BC","",
IF([TransType]="BP",100*[Strike]*[['#Contracts]],
[Cap])))
--------------------
CapDays
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 22
row: 64
value: =IF([SYM]="","",[Cap]*[Days])
--------------------
TotCapDays
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 23
row: 64
value: =IF([SYM]="","",SUMIFS([CapDays],[Trade'#],[[Trade'#]],[Leg],"<="&[Leg]))
--------------------
AROI
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 24
row: 64
value: =IF([TotCapDays],365*[TotPrem]/[TotCapDays],"")
--------------------
BreakEven
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 25
row: 64
value: =IF([SYM]="","",
IF([TransType]="LS",[Strike]-[TotPrem]/[['#Contracts]],
IF([['#Contracts]],[Strike]-[TotPrem]/[['#Contracts]]/100,"")))
--------------------
ActShares
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 26
row: 64
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,"",
IF([TransType]="LS",['#Contracts],
IF([TransType]="AS",100*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="SP",100*[['#Contracts]],
IF([TransType]="BP",100*[['#Contracts]],"")))))
--------------------
ActDate
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 27
row: 64
value: =IF([CloseDate]>0,[CloseDate],
IF([ExpDate]>0,[ExpDate],
TODAY()))
--------------------
Inception
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 28
row: 64
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",[NetPrem]),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",[NetPrem]))
--------------------
1YR
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 29
row: 64
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8 - [ActDate]<366,[NetPrem],"")),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",
IF(TODAY() - [ActDate]<366,[NetPrem],"")))
--------------------
YTD
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 30
row: 64
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],"",
IF(YEAR(PERFORMANCE!D8)=YEAR([ActDate]),[NetPrem],"")),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],"",
IF(YEAR(TODAY())=YEAR([ActDate]),[NetPrem],"")))
--------------------
UnBooked
sheet: <Worksheet "DATA">
column: 31
row: 64
value: =IF(PERFORMANCE!D8>0,
IF(PERFORMANCE!D8<[ActDate],[NetPrem],""),
IF(TODAY()<[ActDate],[NetPrem],""))
--------------------
